<Gmap_id>0x80c2cc66e1bc12af:0xb8a3deec1fe04b82< /Gmap_id><text>After placing an order on this same model of bike in the color "Summer", a week later I was notified that suddenly the bike was out of stock. It wasn‚Äôt out of stock when I ordered it but suddenly it was now. I was disappointed, but they told me they had the bike available in "Misty Blue" and I told them to go ahead and send that one to me. Upon receiving the bike, which was in a LARGE box sitting on my porch after the FedEx guy just dropped it there without notifying me, I opened it up to put it together. There were no assembly instructions to be found. Before you say that I should have taken it to a professional bike mechanic, understand that there is a pandemic and I was pretty confident that I could put it together myself (and it came with tools to assemble it, which implies that you can do it yourself). However, no assembly instructions made this VERY difficult. So I emailed Mr.Bikes and asked if I could have some assembly instructions so I could put my bike together. No response after two days, when they had no problem responding right away when I told them to go ahead and send the bike in a different color. So at that point, I decided to go off of the photo of the bike and common sense and put it together within 3 hours. I must also add that the screw to adjust the seat was too short and had been stripped, so I had to go out and buy a new, longer screw to even be able to ride the bike at my adjusted height. It‚Äôs been a week since emailing them for assembly instructions and still no response. But I certainly got an email asking me to review my purchase.
